    SELECT TOP(1) [g].[ID], [g].[CUSTOM], [g].[DURATION], [g].[END_DATE], [g].[GAMEMASTER_ID], [g].[SCORE], [g].[START_DATE], [g].[TYPE], [g].[WINNER]
    FROM [GAMES] AS [g]
    WHERE [g].[ID] = @__gameId_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g0].[QUESTION_ID], [g0].[GAME_ID], [q].[ID], [q].[ANSWERS], [q].[CATEGORY_ID], [q].[DIFFICULTY_ID], [q].[FIFTY_FIFTY], [q].[GAMEMASTER_ID], [q].[MEDIA], [q].[QUESTION]

    INNER JOIN [QUESTIONS] AS [q] ON [g0].[QUESTION_ID] = [q].[ID]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ID] = [t0].[GAME_ID]
ORDER BY [t].[ID], [t0].[QUESTION_ID], [t0].[GAME_ID]"

""SELECT [t].[ID], [t].[CUSTOM], [t].[DURATION], [t].[END_DATE], [t].[GAMEMASTER_ID], [t].[SCORE], [t].[START_DATE], [t].[TYPE], [t].[WINNER], [t0].[QUESTION_ID], [t0].[GAME_ID], [t0].[ID], [t0].[ANSWERS], [t0].[CATEGORY_ID], [t0].[DIFFICULTY_ID], [t0].[FIFTY_FIFTY], [t0].[GAMEMASTER_ID], [t0].[MEDIA], [t0].[QUESTION]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [g].[ID], [g].[CUSTOM], [g].[DURATION], [g].[END_DATE], [g].[GAMEMASTER_ID], [g].[SCORE], [g].[START_DATE], [g].[TYPE], [g].[WINNER]
    FROM [GAMES] AS [g]
    WHERE [g].[ID] = @__gameId_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g0].[QUESTION_ID], [g0].[GAME_ID], [q].[ID], [q].[ANSWERS], [q].[CATEGORY_ID], [q].[DIFFICULTY_ID], [q].[FIFTY_FIFTY], [q].[GAMEMASTER_ID], [q].[MEDIA], [q].[QUESTION]
    FROM [GAMES_QUESTIONS] AS [g0]
    INNER JOIN [QUESTIONS] AS [q] ON [g0].[QUESTION_ID] = [q].[ID]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ID] = [t0].[GAME_ID]
ORDER BY [t].[ID], [t0].[QUESTION_ID], [t0].[GAME_ID]"
